Central Party and National Government Memorial Week 73

At 9:00 AM on the 8th, the Central Party Headquarters held the 89th Dr. Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week in the Great Hall. Central Committee members Ye Chuqiang, Ma Chaojun, Yu Jingtang, Miao Peicheng, and other officials and guests from various departments and offices, totaling about 560 people, attended. Chairman Ye Chuqiang presided over the ceremony. After the ceremony, the chairman reported briefly that, according to the resolution of the Fourth Plenary Session, the political report will be changed to a speech on Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings and work report every Dr. Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week. The chairman believes that Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings are the only basis for all the work of party members. In the party's doctrines he revealed, we must study with the most sincere spirit at all times and cannot leave it for a day, and we must not abandon our research efforts after the measurement is completed and become lazy. Now, during the period of political tutelage, all government facilities are based on Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings. Once verified, all questions can be answered without much explanation. I have selected several recent matters to briefly report to my comrades: (1) The Executive Yuan issued an order to rectify the academic atmosphere. The main purpose is to enable students to cultivate their character, work hard in their studies, and enable teachers to cultivate their character and encourage their behavior. The deterioration of the school spirit in recent times is due to the background of the reactionaries, who often create rumors that the Kuomintang does not want students to confuse students with weak minds who are easily affected and cannot help but doubt. It must be known that the reactionaries' need for students is very different from what our party wants. The reactionaries want to use students to blindly follow and echo as their tools for reaction, while our party wants students to concentrate on learning and become useful talents for the country, so that they can take on major undertakings in the future. Looking back thirteen years ago, Dr. Sun Yat-sen gave speeches to encourage students in Lingnan, emphasizing that students should concentrate on their studies during their studies and lay the foundation from the root, and his words were extremely earnest. Therefore, this order of the Executive Yuan can also be said to be in memory of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings. (2) The local administration is very inconsistent. There is often a property committee organized in a county, which includes representatives of the county party headquarters, representatives of various district chiefs, representatives of various bureau chiefs, and the county government. The powers are complex and incomprehensible. The party headquarters has the position of supervising the government and has a guiding nature over local administration. The nature of each district and bureau is also different, but they all participate in the organization, which is not in line with the system. Also, there have been cases where the county chief has gathered several county chiefs to hold a meeting to solve a part of the political problems. This method is even more bizarre. When a county's government affairs encounter problems that cannot be solved on its own, it should be submitted to the superior agency for handling. However, they are acting on their own, and the administrative system will be broken by them, which will have a small impact on politics. The central government is rigorously implementing unified politics, and this kind of thing that violates unity must be curbed. The chairman also feels that the central government uses all necessary policies internally and externally and adopts various effective methods to issue orders and decrees. All measures are well-rounded without being confined to formality. In each province and county, local administration must follow a formality, neatly implement the central government's laws and decrees. Even if there are extraordinary talents, they should also be subject to the constraints of laws and decrees and should not go beyond the laws and decrees. Dr. Sun Yat-sen once said in his teachings that all state organs must obey discipline and respect the system, so that politics can have good results. According to this, the above-mentioned organizations that are not in line with the system should undoubtedly be corrected. (3) The lower-level party headquarters feel that it is very difficult to deal with the workers' movement. The workers have always regarded the capitalists as their targets. If the handling is slightly ahead, the workers will leave the party. If lower-level people have problems with the party headquarters, it may lead to labor-capital disputes. Recently, a certain place has a small rope-making industry that is employed by shopkeepers. This kind of industry is very bitter. Although the shopkeepers are slightly more well-off, they are not worth mentioning among the capitalists. However, after the trade union was organized, the first step was to ask for an increase in wages. The shopkeepers thought that this method would force them into bankruptcy, so they would rather let the workers be the shopkeepers and change themselves to be workers. This is really difficult to solve. However, a considerable method can be obtained by examining Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings. 1. The party headquarters should adopt an objective position in the face of the mass movement, assess the situation, and seek a good understanding of the changing situation, without deciding according to its own ideas, resulting in haste. 2. The reason why domestic industry and commerce cannot develop is actually due to the invasion of imperialists. We should broaden our horizons and try to lead the workers to increase domestic production, and we should not simply target domestic capitalists and forget the enemies who are hindering the development of our industry and commerce, etc. After the report, the meeting was adjourned.

On the same morning, at 10:00 AM, the National Government held Dr. Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week. Dai Chuanxian, Song Ziwen, He Yingqin, Wang Boqun, Wang Zhengting, Ma Fuxiang, Liu Ruiheng, Lin Xiang, Zhu Luhe, Chen Yi, Zhou Yawei, Zhang Wohua, Chen Yu, and other officials and staff from the National Government's civil service and military departments, totaling more than 200 people, attended. Chairman Dai Chuanxian presided over the ceremony, and Dai gave a speech until 11:00 AM, when the meeting was adjourned.

Kong Xiangxi Resigns as Minister of Industry 74

The newly appointed Minister of Industry, Kong Xiangxi, submitted to the National Government, saying that he, Xiangxi, had humbly accepted the important task with his humble talent, but was worried about the limitations of his abilities. In the summer of the 17th year, he was ordered to go to Ping Province to see Dr. Sun Yat-sen's coffin and negotiate the post-war affairs in the North. He suffered from enteritis after running around. After the operation, the doctor originally asked him to rest quietly, but because of the responsibilities of his position, he could not relax at all. He continued to work, but unexpectedly, he felt uncomfortable from then on and felt that the arduous task was beyond his capabilities. He repeatedly thought about asking to resign to seek recuperation, but because of repeated rebellions, the party and the country were in trouble, and there was no opportunity to speak out. Since the summer of this year, he has been thinking about the dangerous situation and has suffered from stomach and heart problems. Although he has been repeatedly granted leave to seek treatment, he still recovers and relapses from time to time. According to the doctor, he cannot recover without several months of recuperation. Recently, the military has been pacified and peace has reappeared. The Fourth Plenary Session of this year has been held, and it has been decided to merge the two ministries of agriculture, mining, industry, and commerce into one Ministry of Industry in accordance with the times. Fortunately, from then on, the responsibilities will be lifted and there will be an opportunity to recuperate. It was unexpected that the Central Committee would assign Xiangxi to the Ministry of Industry because he had previously served as Minister of Industry in Guangdong. Upon hearing the order, he was deeply terrified. Thinking back to the beginning of Xiangxi's leadership of industry and commerce, he once followed Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings and the party's policies to formulate administrative guidelines as the standard for measures. Unfortunately, the country has experienced many misfortunes, and the economy is in difficulty. Not only are there many large projects that require funds and are still pending, but even the simple projects have not been fully realized. This is not the intention of the government to set up officials, nor does it violate Xiangxi's devotion to his duties. Every time I think about it, I can't help but walk around the room anxiously and can't sleep. If I were to take on the responsibilities of the entire Ministry of Industry again with my body that has not recovered from a long illness, I would only become more involved in trivial matters and cause more mistakes, and I am afraid that I would fail the Central Committee's intention to work hard for construction. Moreover, at this time when the Central Committee has completed the unification and concentrated talents, it is even more appropriate to give way to wait for the virtuous and capable. Therefore, after thinking again and again, it is better to resign today than to struggle in the future. I humbly and sincerely submit to you, hoping that you will understand my sincerity and withdraw the order, so that I can recuperate with peace of mind. Once I recover, I will still make plans to repay you. I am extremely sincere and awaiting orders.

Zhang Fang's Proposals for Henan Disaster Relief 75

Request to the Central Government for Continued Issuance of Disaster Relief Bonds of Ten Million

Henan's natural disasters are extremely severe, compounded by the ravages of war this summer. The people are displaced and dying, and the Central Plains are almost turned into barren land. Zhang Fang, Chairman of the Henan Disaster Relief Association, has come to Beijing this time to appeal for relief from all parties. He has also drafted five relief proposals to petition the central government. The following is a transcript of the document presented to the National Government: "It is found that Henan Province is located in the Central Plains, connecting several provinces and is known as a region of four battles. It has repeatedly suffered from the scourge of war. Since the ninth year of the Republic, droughts, floods, locust plagues, and hailstorms have occurred frequently. Heavy taxes and levies have exhausted the people's resources, and production has declined daily. The hardship situation in recent years is difficult to describe in words. Just when we were expecting the success of the revolution to free the people from the sea of suffering, unexpected disasters followed one after another, gathering in the Central Plains. The fierceness of this war and the magnitude of the losses are unprecedented catastrophes. All the war zones have been described in detail by the Henan Provincial Disaster Relief Association and Henan people. Now, focusing on the counties most severely affected by the disaster, such as Kaifeng, Chenliu, Qi County, Tongxu, Weishi, Weichuan, Yanling, Zhongmu, Lanfeng, Yu County, Mi County, Shangqiu, Ningling, Sui County, Luyi, Zhecheng, Xihua, Taikang, Kaocheng, Xuchang, Fugou, Linying, Yancheng, Zheng County, Changge, Xiang County, Xingyang, Xingze, Sishui, Tangyin, Xinzheng, Minquan, Luoyang, Yanshi, Gong County, Mengjin, Dengfeng, Linru, Xinan, Mianchi, Baofeng, Yiyang, Pingdengziyou, Shan County, Lingbao, Wenxiang, and other forty-eight counties, a relief plan and estimated funding requirements are formulated as follows, and are hereby submitted for review and speedy implementation to secure the displaced and save the survivors: (1) It is appropriate to establish porridge kitchens and women and children shelters in the above-mentioned counties. It is found that the villages in the war-stricken counties have been reduced to ruins, and the people are displaced. Now, in the severe winter, they are suffering from hunger and cold and are on the verge of death. It is urgent to provide emergency relief to recruit the displaced and extend their lives. It is proposed to set up four shelters and porridge kitchens in each county to accommodate the elderly, weak, women, and children to eat porridge at the factories until the wheat harvest in June next year. A total of forty-eight counties will need 3,000 yuan per month per factory, totaling 4,032,000 yuan. The provision of cotton clothing is not yet included. (2) Fill in war trenches, repair motor roads and the Yellow River dikes to replace relief with labor. It is found that trenches and fortifications within the war zone extend for hundreds of miles, with depths and widths of more than ten feet, destroying tens of thousands of acres of fertile land. It is proposed to investigate separately and retain those that can be used to create ditches for water conservancy. The rest should be filled in using labor as relief within a specified period to restore fertile land, requiring approximately 1,500,000 yuan. At the same time, the motor roads in the war zone should be repaired, from Kaifeng east to Guide and south to Zhoukou, requiring approximately 600,000 yuan. In recent years, the Yellow River dike projects, such as the Liuyuankou and Ligangkou areas, are in imminent danger. It is also necessary to plan for 2,000,000 yuan for major repairs to strengthen the river defenses and relieve the disaster victims. (3) Establish price equalization bureaus to stabilize grain prices. It is found that the soaring grain prices are a cause for concern, especially in the western Henan area. It is proposed to establish price equalization bureaus in multiple locations to purchase large quantities of rice and wheat from Jiangsu, Hubei, and Anhui and set up price equalization to relieve the people's food shortage, requiring approximately 500,000 yuan. (4) Plan to lend cattle, tools, and seeds. It is found that in this war, whether in the front line or in the rear defense counties, cattle and tools have been requisitioned without exception, and food has been completely searched. The sowing season for wheat has already passed. In the blink of an eye, the spring sowing season is approaching, and there is a lack of spring grain seeds, which is also a cause for concern. It is urgent to prepare seeds and cattle tools and lend them to poor farmers so that they can resume farming, requiring approximately 600,000 yuan. (5) Plan to continue to transfer disaster victims to Shandong Province for food. It is found that Henan Province has transferred more than 70,000 disaster victims in recent years. Henan people have obtained food in Shandong Province, which benefits both border defense and people's livelihood. It is still appropriate to prepare large amounts of funds to transfer a large number of people during this disaster, which is a fundamental and essential plan, requiring approximately 1,500,000 yuan. The above-mentioned urgent projects and relief measures are all essential measures at present, and the relief for this winter and next spring has also been taken into consideration. The relief funds required will not be separately raised again. The required relief funds are calculated at the lowest limit, totaling 10,733,000 yuan. I earnestly request that you consider the disaster victims and approve the appropriation or follow the example of issuing public bonds to relieve the Shaanxi disaster and continue to issue public bonds of 10,000,000 yuan specifically for Henan relief. If 5,000,000 yuan can be issued first within the next three months, it can also maintain the proposed plan. Whether it is appropriate or not is respectfully submitted for your decision."

Zhang Xueliang's Situation Passing Through Jinan 76

Jinan Correspondence: Deputy Commander Zhang Xueliang stayed in Beijing this time due to consultations on the aftermath of Northern military affairs, until he left Beijing on the afternoon of the 4th. He crossed the Yangtze River in Pukou and boarded the train, which departed at 8:20 pm. Today (the 5th), he arrived in Jinan at 7:15 pm. Zhang's special train had a total of four carriages. The first carriage was a pilot car, the "Great Wall" armored car, which opened first. The second carriage was a guard car. Zhang's carriage was the third, and the attendant car was the fourth. It was originally scheduled to arrive in Jinan at 5:30 pm today, but the engine was delayed by two hours due to coal loading in Bengbu, so it did not arrive in Jinan until 7:15 pm. The pilot "Great Wall" armored car arrived in Jinan at 6:15 pm, the guard car arrived at 6:45 pm, and the attendant car arrived at 7:45 pm. The provincial government had been informed of Zhang's arrival in Jinan in advance and dispatched military police to guard the station inside and outside. From the station along Pulimen, Daxi Gate, to the provincial government, the posts were densely arranged, and pedestrians were prohibited from passing. Welcoming personnel were required to wear the symbols issued by the provincial government, and even cars passing through were subject to inspection. Around 6 o'clock, the welcoming personnel arrived at the station one after another, including Provincial Chairman Han Fuqu, Civil Affairs Director Li Shuchun, Finance Director Wang Xiangrong, Agriculture and Mining Director Wang Fangting, Construction Director Zhang Honglie, High Court President Wu Zhenzan, 14th Army Commander Cao Fulin, 12th Army Commander Sun Tongxuan, 22nd Division Commander Gu Liangmin, Provincial Committee Zhang Yue, General Headquarters Chief of Staff Li Zongbi, and others, totaling about a hundred people. At 7:15 pm, Zhang's special train entered the station, and the military music played loudly. After the car stopped, Bao Wenwei, the Chief of Staff of the Staff Office, first invited the welcomers to the living room car. Bao said that the Deputy Commander was slightly suffering from stomach problems due to acclimatization in Beijing. Han Fuqu said that he planned to invite the Deputy Commander to rest in Jinan for a few days. Bao said that the Deputy Commander was anxious to return to Liaoning and was afraid that he could not get off the car. Then Zhang immediately went to the living room car from the 15th chartered car and exchanged greetings with the welcomers one by one. Han Fuqu first asked the Deputy Commander if his health was good in Beijing. Zhang replied that it was very good, but he was slightly suffering from stomach problems due to acclimatization. The climate in the central government was excellent, and the various agencies were also working very hard. Han then asked Zhang to get off the car for a rest. Zhang replied that he had stayed in Beijing for too long. Marshal Zhang has been in Liaoning for two months, and Marshal Zhang cannot return to Jilin without my return to Liaoning, so I must hurry back to Liaoning and cannot get off the car. Even in Tianjin, I will only stay for half a day. Today, I saw Ma Shaoyun in Tai'an and wanted to get off the car to climb Mount Tai, but I could not fulfill my wish due to the pursuit of the schedule. I have been to Jinan once before, but I have passed by Tai'an and Qufu twice and did not have time to get off the car. I plan to go to Beijing again in March or April, and I will definitely stay in Shandong for a few days to fulfill my long-cherished wish to climb Mount Tai and visit the Confucius Temple. I heard that the Confucius Temple, Mencius Temple, and Confucius Forest were damaged by artillery fire this time, which is related to the culture of our country and is watched by both Chinese and foreigners, so we should raise funds to repair it as soon as possible. Han asked if Commander-in-Chief Jiang had left. Zhang replied that he was scheduled to go to Jiujiang this morning. Han asked how the aftermath of Shanxi was. Zhang replied that Yan had arrived in Tianjin and lived in the Japanese concession. Although Feng knew that he had left Jin, he still did not know where he was going. He had already telegraphed Shang Qiyu to entrust him to inquire about Feng's intentions. Originally, I had already agreed with Commander-in-Chief Jiang to earnestly telegraph Yan Feng to guarantee his safety for his resignation and going abroad. Han said that Shi Hanzhang is now waiting in Tianjin for the Deputy Commander. In the future, Mr. Feng (Yuxiang) and Hanzhang will rely on the Deputy Commander's great efforts to mediate. Zhang replied that he would do his best to protect their safety. He also asked about the situation in Shandong. Han replied that it was still calm, but there were local bandits in southern Shandong, and the Third Route Army had sent a brigade to encircle them together with Ma Shaoyun's troops. Zhang asked if Sun Lianzhong's troops had arrived. Han replied that the troops arrived in Caozhou on the 2nd and Jining on the 3rd. Zhang nodded again and again. Han said that Shandong affairs all rely on the Deputy Commander's guidance. Zhang said that there was no need to be polite. At this point in the conversation, the welcomers got off the car, leaving only Han in the car. After another five minutes of conversation, Han got off the car. At 7:15 pm, the guard car headed north first (the pilot "Great Wall" armored car stayed in Jinan and did not go north with it). At 7:45 pm, Zhang's special train headed north amidst the music and farewell. Zhang stood outside the car door and nodded to the welcomers as a courtesy. The attendant car headed north at 8:15 pm. Those who escorted the car included She Xu, Director of the Jinpu Railway Car Affairs Office, Li Guozhou, Director of the Locomotive General Section, Gu Qiwen, Zhang Yuanhe, etc. (Evening of December 5th)

Feng and Yan's Whereabouts After Leaving Shanxi 77

Feng Secretly Arrives in Suiyuan and Enters Kulun

Yan Disguised Passes Through Datong and Goes to Tianjin

Taiyuan Correspondence: The news of Feng's departure from Shanxi has been rumored for a long time. Feng secretly left Jin on the 25th of last month. It is reported that Feng arrived in Suiyuan the day after he left Jin and made some arrangements there. On the 28th, he took two cars with two Russian translators and two followers and went north to Russia via Kulun. Due to the difficulty of the journey, the followers he brought were also simplified. As for whether he will recuperate in Russia or transfer to Europe, there is no news at this time. According to a friend who returned from Suiyuan, Feng's whereabouts were extremely secret this time. After arriving in Suiyuan, he ordered all the followers to change into plain clothes. Although he stayed in Suiyuan for two days, no one outside knew about it. Only after he left did the outside world know a little about it. It is conceivable how secret his whereabouts were.

After Yan received Zhang Xueliang's telegram guaranteeing his safety along the way, he was determined to leave Jin. However, at that time, for Yan's safety, the official kept secret the exact time of Yan's departure. Some said that he had indeed left on the 30th of last month, and some said that he only left yesterday. According to reliable news, Yan did indeed leave on the night of the 29th of last month in disguise (wearing a Western suit) with three followers in two cars and secretly went north to Datong. He then took a passenger car on the PingSui Railway to Ping and transferred to Tianjin. Zhao Daiwen received a telegram in Wutai that Yan had safely arrived in Tianjin, and only then did he telegraph Shang Zhen yesterday to ask him to telegraph the Central Government and Deputy Commander Zhang to report and notify all agencies in the city. At the same time, he also sent a special commissioner to Shijiazhuang to ask Wang Shuchang's Chen Chief of Staff and Yu Xuezhong's Chief of Staff, who had been sent by Pingjin to meet Yan, not to come to Jin. After Shang received the telegram, he immediately complied, and the news of Yan Feng's departure from Jin, which had been rumored for many days, came to an end.

Since Yan and Feng have left Jin one after another, the most important issue after that is naturally to handle the aftermath. It is reported that Shang Zhen, Xu Yongchang, and others are currently deliberating on the distribution of military pay, the reorganization of finance, the reorganization of troops, and the division of defense areas in order to discuss them with Deputy Commander Zhang one by one (December 2nd).

Communist Party Organizations Repeatedly Crushed in Hunan Province 78

Many Important Figures Captured

Changsha Correspondence: Although the Communist bandits in various parts of Hunan Province have been defeated separately, the Communist Party members are still lurking and thinking of acting, secretly forming organizations in an attempt to sabotage the Changsha Fortress, electric light yarn factories, and instigate students, workers, soldiers to organize reactionary groups to expand the riot plan. After strict investigation by the Rural Clearing Headquarters, several pseudo-provincial, county, and municipal organizations were recently cracked down in the provincial capital and Matang Jinggang and other places in Changsha County, and many important figures were captured. Yesterday, He Jian telegraphed to the Central Government to report the situation of cracking down on the Communist Party organizations as follows: "The Communist bandits who previously invaded the province were severely suppressed by the troops and various armies, and although they fled in different directions, the Communist Party members still tried to make trouble and secretly formed organizations. After strict investigation by the sent teams, several pseudo-provincial, county, and municipal organizations were recently cracked down in the provincial capital and Matang Jinggang and other places in Changsha County, and Liu Shaoqing, the wife of Wang Shoudao, the pseudo-provincial committee member, Liu Huilan, the wife of Yu Muming, the pseudo-provincial committee member, and Ou Zhenfan, Lin Youxin, Peng Daosheng and other key criminals, the pseudo-municipal and county committee members, were captured, and many pseudo-central, provincial, municipal, and county notices and reactionary publications were seized. The contents of the pseudo-notices are extremely cunning for sabotaging the Changsha Fortress, electric light yarn factories, and instigating students, workers, soldiers to organize reactionary groups to expand the riot plan. After interrogation, the responsible key bandits also confessed that they were ordered to set up organizations in secret organizations in an attempt to directly attack Changsha and invade Wuhan. In addition to handling the captured Communist bandits in accordance with the law, we have also sent letters to the military and political organs to strictly guard against them. He Jian, Commander of Hunan Rural Clearing, kowtows and thanks the seal."

Liaoning Province Decides to Issue Prize-Winning Bonds 79

Establishment of the Six-Percent Bond Committee

Shenyang Correspondence: In recent years, the financial situation in the Northeast has been tight, and local industries have seen depression. As a result, many merchants and farmers from various counties have come to the province to request loans for turnover. There are as many as forty county groups making this request. Among them, some have petitioned the provincial government's Finance Department, and some have contacted the Chamber of Commerce and various banks. The Liaoning legal groups previously planned to issue prize-winning bonds to relieve merchants and farmers, which was approved by the chairman of the province, Zang Shiyi. A meeting was held in the provincial government to discuss this matter. In addition to Chairman Zang, Chen Wenxue, Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, Liu Heling, Director of the Department of Agriculture and Mining, Peng Xiangting, President of the Bank of the Three Eastern Provinces, Lu Muting, General Manager, Wang Huayi, President of the Education Association, Ji Jinsheng, President of the Chamber of Commerce and Industry, Jin Zhechen, and Huang Heng Hao, representatives from the Department of Finance, etc. After a long discussion on the importance of the matter, the following resolutions were made: (1) It is proposed to issue bonds of 20,000,000 yuan with a monthly interest rate of six percent, paid every four months and recovered in three years. (2) First, a Liaoning Six-Percent Bond Committee will be organized by various agencies and legal groups to carry out various matters. Zang Shiyi, the chairman of the province, was elected as the chairman of the committee. (3) There are many difficulties in printing bonds. Due to time constraints, it was decided to use the 100-yuan Feng banknotes of the official bank that were not signed as 2-yuan bonds, signed and stamped for identification. (4) The various conditions will be telegraphed by Chairman Zang to Deputy Commander Zhang for approval and submitted to the Northeast Political Committee for approval before implementation. (5) The loan method will be handled by the official banks in each county, with one supervisor in each county to prevent local tyrants and evil gentry from profiting from it. If there is any usury or exploitation, they will be severely punished. (6) These bonds are universally applicable to officials, merchants, and farmers. The Finance Department and various tax bureaus will also accept them for tax collection (December 2nd).

Trend of Timber Merchants in Chuzhou Resisting Levies 80

The Department of Finance Increases Timber Levies Threefold

All Timber Merchants Go on Strike for Two Months

More Than Ten Thousand Workers Lose Their Jobs

Hangzhou Correspondence: Chuzhou in eastern Zhejiang is located in the mountains and is a hub for the production of timber. Among the ten subordinate counties, Longquan, Qingyuan, and Jingning are the most famous. The annual sales to Ouhang and the Yangtze River Basin are worth about six to seven million gold. The people rely on this income to exchange cloth and rice to support their lives. However, in recent years, due to the impact of war and Communist bandits, they have suffered huge losses, both tangible and intangible, and their livelihoods have become increasingly difficult. Local business groups are planning to provide relief to alleviate the people's difficulties. Unexpectedly, the Department of Finance ordered the United Taxation Bureaus of Qingtian, Lishui, and Longquan to increase the timber levy in order to increase tax revenue. When the timber merchants heard this, they were all alarmed and at a loss. For this reason, they stopped transporting timber to seek resistance. So far, it has been nearly two months, and more than ten thousand workers have lost their jobs. The source of economic income is about to be cut off, and the cash shops and commercial shops have shown signs of poor turnover. If a solution is not found quickly, the social security and people's livelihood will be a cause for concern. The process is recorded as follows:

Reasons for Increasing the Levy: It is found that the United Taxation Bureaus of Longquan, Lishui, and Qingtian rely entirely on timber as the main source of tax collection. The Department of Finance needs funds urgently and has increased the quota of each bureau every year.

Page 8

The former Director of the Qingtian United Taxation Bureau, Guo, resigned on the pretext of a tax revenue shortfall. The vacant position was taken over by Qu Dasan. Director Qu realized that the previous director's collection was not strong, so he increased the timber levy, completely overturning the established case of extracting five per thousand for more than ten years and 3.9 li per piece. He submitted a request to the Department of Finance to increase the levy rate. The Department of Finance immediately instructed to approve it, and the same was true for the Longquan and Lishui Bureaus, which inevitably had a knock-on effect. As a result, the announcement of the increased levy was posted all over the streets.

The Situation of Stopping Transportation: Timber merchants in Longquan, Qingyuan, and Jingning believe that at this time when the cut in the likin is about to be realized, there is suddenly an increase in the levy. Regardless of the cost of the timber, the original tax of 3 fen for white timber has been increased by 9 fen, and the original tax of 4.5 li for pine timber and miscellaneous wood has been increased by 1 jiao and 2 fen. The levy rate has been increased by three times according to the original tax, becoming a levy rate of 15 or 20 per thousand, which is considered to be in great conflict with the payment of inland tax regulations and is difficult to accept. Therefore, they unanimously stopped transporting timber as a passive resistance. The timber stacked along the river is increasing by tens of thousands every day, and the loss is conceivable.

The Process of Petitioning: In addition to implementing the stop of transportation, the timber merchants also demanded that the chambers of commerce in the respective places discuss countermeasures. After the chambers of commerce and timber merchants described their various hardships, they separately petitioned the Ministry of Finance and the Department of Finance to allow the electricity to be ordered to collect taxes as before in order to maintain the established case. On the one hand, they elected representatives Liu Yucheng, Li Zhongxian, etc. to go to the province to petition. As a result, the Department of Finance only allowed personnel to thoroughly investigate and deliberate on the matter again. The representatives believed that the purpose had not been achieved and planned to go to Beijing to continue petitioning.

Now the Department of Finance has specially appointed Yao Chong to conduct a thorough investigation due to the firm opposition of the timber merchants and promised to have the power to mediate according to the situation. Therefore, when Yao arrived in Qingtian, he deeply understood the inside story of various kinds, and then formulated a compromise plan. The timber merchants could not afford to bear the increase of 9 fen of tax, and it would be detrimental to the government's prestige if no increase was made at all. Approximately, at least 2 fen must be added as a transitional step. He has sought the opinions of the timber merchants' representatives on this matter, but the representatives insisted that the order must be completely revoked, so Yao is still lingering in Qingtian, engaged in dredging.

Full Text of the Civil Code Relatives Part (3) (Continued) 81

Passed by the Legislative Yuan in the Third Reading

(Article One Thousand and Twenty-Eight) When the wife dies, the wife's original property shall belong to her heirs. If there is a deficiency, the husband shall compensate for it, but only to the extent that the deficiency arises from a cause attributable to the husband.

(Article One Thousand and Twenty-Nine) When the husband dies, the wife shall recover her original property. If there is a deficiency, she may request compensation from the husband's heirs.

(Article One Thousand and Thirty) The division of joint property shall, unless otherwise stipulated, allow the wife to recover her original property. If there is a deficiency, the husband or his heirs shall bear it, but this shall not apply if the deficiency arises from a cause attributable to the wife.

Section Three: Contractual Property Systems, Subsection One: Joint Property System

(Article One Thousand and Thirty-One) The property and income of the husband and wife, except for separate property, shall be merged into joint property, which shall be jointly owned by the husband and wife. Neither party may dispose of their respective share of the joint property.

(Article One Thousand and Thirty-Two) The joint property shall be managed by the husband, and the expenses of management shall be borne by the joint property.

(Article One Thousand and Thirty-Three) When one spouse disposes of joint property, the consent of the other spouse should be obtained, but this shall not apply to dispositions necessary for management. The lack of consent in the preceding paragraph may not be asserted against a third party, unless the third party knew or should have known of the lack of consent, or the circumstances indicate that the property belongs to the joint property.

(Article One Thousand and Thirty-Four) The following debts shall be the responsibility of the husband personally and shall be paid out of the joint property: 1. Debts incurred by the husband before marriage. 2. Debts incurred by the husband during the marriage relationship. 3. Debts arising from the wife's acting as an agent as provided in Article One Thousand and Five. 4. Debts incurred by the wife during the marriage relationship as a burden on the joint property, except as provided in the preceding paragraph.

(Article One Thousand and Thirty-Five) The following debts shall be the responsibility of the wife personally and shall be paid out of the joint property: 1. Debts incurred by the wife before marriage. 2. Debts arising from the wife's occupation or business. 3. Debts arising from the wife's inherited property. 4. Debts arising from the wife's tortious acts.

(Article One Thousand and Thirty-Six) The following debts shall be the responsibility of the wife to be paid only out of her separate property: 1. Debts secured by the wife's separate property. 2. Debts arising from the wife's actions exceeding the scope of agency power under Article One Thousand and Five.

(Article One Thousand and Thirty-Seven) If the joint property is insufficient to cover household living expenses, the wife shall also be personally responsible.

(Article One Thousand and Thirty-Eight) If a debt of the joint property is paid with the joint property, there shall be no right of reimbursement between the husband and wife. If a debt of the joint property is paid with separate property, or a debt of the separate property is paid with the joint property, there is a right of reimbursement, which may be claimed even during the marriage relationship.

(Article One Thousand and Thirty-Nine) When one spouse dies, half of the joint property shall belong to the heirs of the deceased, and the other half shall belong to the surviving spouse. If the allocation of the property in the preceding paragraph is otherwise agreed upon, the agreement shall prevail. In the situation in the first paragraph, if the surviving spouse is not legally entitled to be an heir, the amount of joint property they may claim shall not exceed the amount they would have received at the time of divorce.

(Article One Thousand and Forty) When the joint property relationship is extinguished, unless otherwise provided by law or contract, each spouse shall receive half of the joint property.

(Article One Thousand and Forty-One) The husband and wife may agree by contract that only income shall be joint property. The property earned by the husband and wife through labor during the marriage relationship and the profits from the original property shall be the income under the preceding paragraph and shall be subject to the provisions regarding the joint property system. The original property belonging to the husband and wife at the time of marriage and during the marriage relationship shall be subject to the provisions regarding the statutory property system.

Subsection Two: Unified Property System

(Article One Thousand and Forty-Two) The husband and wife may agree by contract to estimate the value of the wife's property, excluding separate property, and transfer ownership to the husband, and obtain the right to claim repayment of the estimated value.

(Article One Thousand and Forty-Three) The provisions regarding the statutory property system shall apply mutatis mutandis to unified property, except as provided in the preceding article.

Subsection Three: Separate Property System

(Article One Thousand and Forty-Four) Under separate property, each spouse retains ownership, management rights, and rights of use and benefit over their property.

(Article One Thousand and Forty-Five) If the wife entrusts the management of her property to the husband, it is presumed that the husband has the right to use the income from the property to pay for household living expenses. The wife may revoke the management right at any time. The right of revocation may not be waived.

(Article One Thousand and Forty-Six) The following debts shall be the responsibility of the husband to pay: 1. Debts incurred by the husband before marriage. 2. Debts incurred by the husband during the marriage relationship. 3. Debts arising from the wife's acting as an agent as provided in Article One Thousand and Five.

(Article One Thousand and Forty-Seven) The following debts shall be the responsibility of the wife to pay: 1. Debts incurred by the wife before marriage. 2. Debts incurred by the wife during the marriage relationship. Debts incurred by the husband and wife for household living expenses shall be borne by the wife if the husband is unable to pay.

(Article One Thousand and Forty-Eight) The husband may request the wife to bear a reasonable share of household living expenses.

Section Five: Divorce

(Article One Thousand and Forty-Nine) If both husband and wife consent to a divorce, they may divorce themselves, but a minor must obtain the consent of their legal representative.

(Article One Thousand and Fifty) A divorce by mutual consent shall be in writing and shall be signed by two or more witnesses.

(Article One Thousand and Fifty-One) After a divorce by mutual consent, the husband shall be responsible for the custody of the children, unless otherwise agreed upon.

(Article One Thousand and Fifty-Two) One spouse may petition the court for divorce only if the other spouse has one of the following circumstances: 1. Bigamy. 2. Adultery. 3. One spouse has been subjected to abuse by the other spouse that makes it impossible to live together. 4. The wife has abused or has been abused by the husband's direct ascendants, making it impossible to live together. 5. One spouse has maliciously abandoned the other spouse in a continuous state. 6. One spouse intends to kill the other spouse. 7. Having an incurable malignant disease. 8. Having a serious and incurable mental illness. 9. Having been missing for more than three years. 10. Being sentenced to imprisonment for more than three years or being sentenced to imprisonment for committing a dishonorable crime.

(Article One Thousand and Fifty-Three) A party with the right to claim based on the circumstances in Article One Thousand and Fifty-Two, Paragraph One or Paragraph Two, may not petition for divorce if they have consented in advance, condoned after the fact, or have known about it for more than six months, or if more than two years have passed since the occurrence of the circumstances.

(Article One Thousand and Fifty-Four) A party with the right to claim based on the circumstances in Article One Thousand and Fifty-Two, Paragraph Six and Paragraph Ten, may not petition for divorce if more than one year has passed since they became aware of it, or if more than five years have passed since the occurrence of the circumstances.

(Article One Thousand and Fifty-Five) In the case of a divorce by judgment, the provisions of Article One Thousand and Fifty-One shall apply to the custody of children, but the court may appoint a guardian for the benefit of the children.

(Article One Thousand and Fifty-Six) If one spouse suffers damages as a result of a divorce judgment, they may claim compensation from the other spouse who is at fault. In the situation of the preceding paragraph, even if the damage is not of a property nature, the injured party may claim a reasonable amount of compensation, but only if the injured party is not at fault. The right to claim in the preceding paragraph may not be assigned or inherited, unless it has been promised by contract or a lawsuit has been filed.

(Article One Thousand and Fifty-Seven) If one spouse who is not at fault is facing financial hardship as a result of a divorce judgment, the other spouse shall provide a reasonable amount of alimony, even if the other spouse is not at fault.

(Article One Thousand and Fifty-Eight) When a husband and wife divorce, regardless of the marital property system they originally used, each shall recover their inherent property. If there is a deficiency, the husband shall bear it, but this shall not apply if the deficiency arises from a cause not attributable to the husband.

(To be continued)

Suzhou 83

Water Police Officer Reports Robbery of Opium Case: Zhu Youlin, the former leader of the Sixth Third Squad of the Wuxi Water Police, fled after robbing thirty-six dan of opium in the Goose Town waters at the intersection of Suzhou and Wuxi. The Wuxi County Government has repeatedly issued wanted notices without success. Yang Bingsheng, an officer of the local unit, yesterday (the 8th) submitted a report to the High Court, accusing Zhu Youlin of robbing thirty-six dan of opium, which he then transported to Shanghai and sold for tens of thousands of yuan. He used one thousand yuan to bribe District Chief Mao Shouchang, who then allowed him to escape. He is currently hiding in Tianjin, etc., and requested a thorough investigation, the issuance of a wanted notice, arrest, and legal action.

Robbery and Injury Case Occurs in Downtown Area: Chen Wangshi, a resident of No. 19, First Gate, Guanqian Palace Lane, went out shopping the evening before last, around 7:00 PM, and was returning home. When she reached the gate, because her hands were full of food, she was unable to open the door. A stranger saw a gold bracelet on Chen Wangshi's arm and came forward, pretending to be helpful, to open the door. Taking advantage of Chen Wangshi's inattentiveness, he robbed her of the gold bracelet and fled. Chen Wangshi immediately shouted for help. Han Xueliang, a vendor selling sesame cakes who was coming towards her, saw the robber looking flustered and stepped forward to arrest him. However, the two collided violently and fell to the ground. The robber then pulled out a sharp blade and stabbed Han Xueliang in the shoulder. The robber ultimately escaped. The patrol officer and police officers from the Second Branch and Third Precinct went out to search for the robber, but he was nowhere to be found.

Mirror Pavilion Ruins to be Rebuilt as Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall: The Mirror Treasure Pavilion of Xuanmiao Temple was destroyed by fire in the early years of the Republic of China, and there have been no resources to rebuild it since then. Now, the Wu County Party Consolidation Committee and the County Government, in memory of the late Premier Sun Yat-sen, have decided to rebuild the ruins of the Mirror Treasure Pavilion as the Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall. The Wu County Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall Preparatory Committee has been established, consisting of Party Consolidation Committee member Wang Jianwen, District Chief Shen Weikui of the Third Public Security District, County Magistrate Huang Yunzhen, Finance Bureau Chief Yuan Xiaogu, Public Security Bureau Chief Bu Jing, Construction Bureau Chief Wei Zumo, Police Team Captain Du Hongyi, Education Bureau Chief Wu Yaozhang, High Court President Lin Biao, District Court President Hu Yuanchun, and local gentry Zhang Yuntuan, and 19 others. A meeting will be convened on the 13th of this month to discuss the direction of progress.

Wuxi 84

Widening of Sheqiao Road for Automobile Traffic: The entire length of Sheqiao Road, west of Huinong Bridge outside Guangfu Gate in this county, is 2,400 feet long. However, the road itself is unusually narrow and prone to low-lying areas during rainy weather, making transportation very inconvenient. Therefore, local people initiated a renovation project, and together with the Huishang Township Public Office, submitted a request to the First District Public Office for filing and requested the County Construction Bureau to issue a road construction permit. Xiao Hongyou contracted the project, which began the other day to widen the road surface by five feet in preparation for automobile traffic. It is scheduled to be completed within three weeks.

Ministry Appoints Committee to Investigate Consumption Tax: The Fourth Plenary Session of this year decided to implement the reduction of "li" [a small unit of currency] by replacing it with a special consumption tax managed by the Ministry of Finance, starting on January 1 of the 20th year [of the Republic, i.e., 1931]. Preparations are currently underway, and it is planned to conduct trial runs on silk, cocoons, oil, tea, paper, wood, and ceramics first. Yesterday, Ministry Committee members Li Pengshou and Jiang Chensheng came to Wuxi from Beijing and went to various industries to conduct investigations. The Chamber of Commerce, considering that this matter is closely related to improving the tax law and the commerce itself, specifically invited representatives from related industries to a meeting this afternoon (the 9th) to discuss the matter and solicit opinions.

Planning the Organization of the Jiangsu Provincial Maritime Public Security Bureau: Jiangsu Provincial Chairman Ye Chucang, at the beginning of his tenure, in view of the rampant banditry in the counties north and south of the Yangtze River, planned to organize the Jiangsu Provincial Maritime Public Security Bureau immediately in order to assist the land police in their dedicated work of suppressing bandits. However, due to financial difficulties, it was temporarily suspended. Recently, he received a handwritten order from Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, ordering him to organize and establish it as soon as possible, and to be especially cautious in selecting the director. At that time, Jiang Chaoxiong, the director of the Fifth District of the Maritime Public Security, led his team to encircle and suppress bandits in Qingjiang and Siyang, killing countless bandits and killing the pseudo-brigade commander Xue Changhuai. The banditry in the county was gradually quelled, and his merits were outstanding. It has now been decided to appoint Jiang Chaoxiong as the Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Maritime Public Security Bureau. He will immediately prepare for the organization and is determined to establish it in the shortest possible time.

Yang Guanchang Kidnapped in Shanghai: Yang Guanchang, the former manager of the Yükang Yarn Factory in Zhoushanbang, went to Shanghai at the end of last month to attend the funeral of Xue Liquan, residing at the Zhenhua Hotel. Later, because his friend Mr. Sun was getting married at Yipinxian, Yang also went to offer his congratulations. Since then, his whereabouts have been unknown. His family has been searching everywhere for several days without any trace. Recently, his family suddenly received an anonymous letter demanding 10,000 yuan for ransom and specifying a location. His family has not yet come up with a solution.

Five Robbers Captured in Taibo Township Robbery Case: The home of Weng Qixian, a resident of Quejiaqiao Village, Qin Village Township, Twelfth District (Taibo Township), was robbed by more than ten bandits at around 1:00 AM on the 2nd of this month, resulting in a loss of more than one thousand yuan. The other day, County Government Political Police Chief Wu Zhengrong received a confidential report stating that several robbers involved in the case were hiding in the Meicun area. Police Chief Wu immediately led detectives and informants to the countryside to make arrests. Five robbers were captured on the spot and escorted to the city. Police Chief Wu interrogated the robbers, and one of them was found to be unrelated to the case. The other four were strongly suspected of involvement. Yesterday, a document was prepared and transferred to the County Government for investigation and handling.

Changzhou 85

Bandit Leader from Xinghua Arrested in Changzhou: Wang Zhaocai, a bandit leader from Xinghua County, had escaped to Changzhou after committing a crime of escorting prisoners in Jiangbei. He hid in a boat anchored near Ganshuyan for a long time. During the day, he pretended to be fishing, but at night, he continued his career as a bandit. He had accumulated some savings and was privately minting money and opening a hall to recruit disciples. Recently, he planned to open a large incense hall at the Dongyuehe Tea House outside the city. At around 1:00 PM on the 7th, he was gathering with his accomplices at the Changle Tea House on Renyu Bridge in the city when he was detected by police detectives. The detectives immediately returned to the team to report, and police officers were dispatched. Wang Zhaocai was leaving the tea house when he was identified by a detective and arrested. He was taken to the team for interrogation and handling.

Villager in Fenghuang Township Beats Wife to Death: Shi Shengtai, the fifth son of the Shi family in Minghuang Town, Old Huihua Township, Wuyi, named Fuxiang, married the daughter of Zhou Zengxiang from Nanzhou Village. Initially, the couple was very affectionate, but recently, Fuxiang had been gambling at home and lost more than eighty yuan. He wanted to sell the land, but the land deed was kept at his uncle's house. The other day, he asked his wife to return to her parents' home to retrieve the land deed, but his wife refused. Inadvertently, he kicked his wife hard, hitting a vital point. She immediately fell to the ground and died. Afterwards, Shi's father sent his son to the Seventh Public Security Bureau for custody on the 7th, and the Seventh District Public Office reported the matter to the County Court Prosecutor's Office, which dispatched personnel to the countryside to conduct an examination for verification.

Pinghu 86

The Zhong Case Involves Transfer of Jurisdiction: The case of Yang Daochang, the captain of the County Government Patrol Team, being accused by Zhong Weidang in Shuyuan Alley of financial fraud, was reopened for continued hearing by the County Government yesterday (the 6th) at 3:00 PM. First, Zhong's housekeeper Wang Pinshu and Ge Yuwen, Yao Kecheng, Chu Ma, and others were interrogated. Yang Daochang's testimony was the same as before, consistently denying the charges. Then, County Magistrate Shen summoned all members of the patrol team and laborers to stand in two rows on the open space outside the courtroom, and ordered Wang Pinshu and the other four to identify one by one whether any of them had come to the Zhong family to extort money the other day. The result was that none of them were identified. Thereupon, the court declared that the defendant in this case was a member of the County Government and, according to law, should be presented to the High Court to designate a nearby court for transfer of jurisdiction. The County Government's handling of this case would conclude today. After the pronouncement, the defendant requested an examination of Zhong Weixuan's opium addiction. The hearing officer replied that this was another matter and rejected the request. Today (the 7th) at 3:00 PM, Zhong Weixuan invited forty to fifty local gentry to a meeting to discuss countermeasures.

Huzhou 87

Banditry in Changxing Becomes More Rampant: In the Changxing County area under the jurisdiction of Huzhou, incidents of kidnapping and looting have been heard of daily since summer. Although the military and police have been carrying out suppression efforts, scattered bandits are present everywhere. Yin Aiqiao, who lives in Hanjiadian, a place more than ten miles away from the county seat, is a well-to-do person who was targeted by bandits. At about 10:00 PM on the 4th of this month, more than twenty bandits suddenly came, speaking with a 客音 [Hakka or other southern dialect], each carrying shoulder poles, knives, and sticks, and broke down the door. They looted all the clothes and bedding and more than ten stones of rice, causing a loss of more than 400 yuan. Furthermore, the ship sailing from Changxing to Hexi the other day, when departing from Changxing, saw dozens of bandits holding guns and speaking a 外音 [foreign sounding or local dialect] on the shore, shouting for it to stop. Seeing the situation, the crew had no choice but to stop. Two bandits guarded the shore while the remaining bandits boarded the ship. The passengers were searched one by one, with no one spared. After about an hour, the bandits went ashore. An examination afterwards revealed that passengers' clothing, silver, and goods worth about 300 yuan were looted.

Fengxian 88

Chamber of Commerce Members Limited Time Registration: The Nangiao and Zhuangxing Chambers of Commerce were ordered to be abolished by both the Party and government due to illegal reorganization, and merchants from various industries were convened to discuss reorganization. Now, it is known that this case has been handed over to the Training Department, which plans to first register and review the original members of the two associations in terms of organization, and solicit new members to join the association in order to start preparing for the establishment of industry associations. Therefore, the department has already proposed Shen Kechang, Yang Xiyuan, and Sun Pinquan as Chamber of Commerce member registrars. It was passed and appointed by the current association, and registration must be completed within one month in accordance with the law.

Large Number of Bandits Request Instructions for Execution: Recently, due to the frequent banditry cases in various districts and the fact that less than three out of ten are solved, the County Government specifically ordered the County Police Team to arrest the perpetrators within a time limit. Warrants were issued for the main criminals and rewards were offered to encourage them. In addition to the bandit leader Shen Ayou, who was previously captured and ordered to be executed on the spot in Nangiao as a warning to the public, several more robbers have been captured in the Qixianqiao and Shenzhang robbery cases in recent days: Xu Amei, Xue Xiemei, Wei Amao, Wang Xiaodi, Fei Jinxiang, and Xu Jinxiang, who makes clothes, Amao, Ji Aqiu, and Xu Jinxu (with a fake passport of Zhou Chengxi found), who was captured on the spot by the gate police at the gate of the County Government in the Zhang Mengjun and Li Shengpu family robbery case in Sanguantang, etc. More than ten people have been interrogated, and they have confessed to the facts. Therefore, County Magistrate Shen Qingchen wired the Provincial Government yesterday to request instructions for the execution of the criminals in accordance with the Regulations for the Punishment of Bandits, distinguishing between principals and accomplices.

Nantong 89

Reorganization of the Journalists Association: Due to the increase in the number of newspapers, the Nantong Journalists Association reorganized on the 7th and elected seven executive committee members: Zhang Qingyu, Sun Zizai, Cai Guohua, Shao Boyan, Yi Zongliu, Wu Jianzhang, and Lü Pinxian were elected. It was resolved that all newspapers would suspend publication for one week from January 2nd to 8th.

Thorough Investigation of Purchase of Firearms: All districts in Tongyi are in turmoil due to banditry. The firearms for the self-defense groups are purchased by the County Government, totaling 2,000 pieces. The Civil Affairs Department ordered the county to pay 145 yuan per piece, but the County Government sold them for 200 yuan per piece. There is a public outcry, and a thorough investigation is currently underway.

Executive Committee of the Education Association Elected: The Nantong County Education Association held an executive committee meeting on the 7th and elected members of the standing committee. Xiao Qiu was elected.

Yangzhou 90

Superintendent Zhang Scheduled to Arrive in Yangzhou: Jiangsu Provincial Pacification Superintendent Zhang Zhijiang has been in office for many days. His superintendent's office has long been surveyed and determined to be the He Family Garden in Diaojia Lane in this city. However, this house was originally the headquarters of the 133rd Brigade. In addition to Superintendent Zhang having been approved by the Commander-in-Chief's Headquarters to send Chief Military Law Officer Li Gongjian to Yangzhou to take charge of everything, Chief of Staff Mai Mou and Yu Junshi also came to Yangzhou the other day to assist in the arrangement. It is said that Superintendent Zhang will come north before the 20th of this month. Therefore, the office is working day and night to construct and repair.

Trouble Arises During Opium Arrests: The Tenth Public Security Bureau of Huangjueqiao in this county arrested six opium offenders in its jurisdiction yesterday (the 6th). The son of a local township head, Guo, was also among those arrested, causing trouble at that time. Hundreds of people gathered inside and outside the bureau, creating a threatening atmosphere, eager to snatch back the opium offenders. As a result, three of the arrested opium offenders were snatched back. Subsequently, Zhang Shiqiu, the director of the branch, came to the city to report the situation. Director Liao of the Public Security Bureau was informed and at the same time, Township Head Guo also came to the city to report to the Public Security Bureau. Chief Inspector Liao has now been assigned by the Director of the Public Security Bureau to send Patrol Officer Huang Jinting and Police Officer Li from the Fourth Resident Station in this city to welcome and bring the three opium offenders who are in custody to the city for further verification.

Gaoyou 91

Huikang Money Shop to Cease Operations: Ding Shaoan, the manager of Huikang Money Shop outside the North Gate of this city, specifically convened a shareholders' meeting on the 4th. Unexpectedly, all shareholders held a negative attitude and unanimously agreed to cease operations. Wu Mingqi, the shop's resident clerk in the town, came to Gaoyou last night (the 5th) to help clear the accounts. It is reported that the losses are minimal when offsetting deposits and debts.

Master Commits Suicide, Loyal Dog Cries for Help: Huang Defa, a peddler from Youjiazhuang in this county, went to Yangzhou to sell fruit the other day. Due to the poor market conditions in the county, he lost dozens of yuan, which caused him much distress. He hanged himself yesterday morning. Unexpectedly, the dog he kept suddenly barked frantically in front of the door. The neighbors were very surprised and went inside to see that Huang had hanged himself. They immediately came forward to rescue him, and he was able to regain consciousness.

Changsha Year-End Closure Extended: Changsha has been repeatedly looted by the Guizhou rebels and the communist bandits, and commerce has been sluggish. With the government promoting the Gregorian calendar, it is particularly difficult to close the year-end accounts on time. It is reported that various commercial groups have mostly resolved to extend the closure period to the day before the Beginning of Spring.
