Robbery of Commercial Press Wages 162

Totaling Three Thousand Seven Hundred Yuan

In recent years, the business of the Commercial Press factory on Baoshan Road in Zhabei has been thriving. A second factory was specially set up across from the Guangdong Merchants Hospital on Tiantong An Road. All employees' wages were sent there monthly by a staff member. The day before yesterday at 3:00 PM, a staff member was carrying paper money totaling 3,700 yuan in a private car to distribute it at the factory. When he reached the corner of Zhongxing Road and Baotong Road, four robbers suddenly appeared, each holding a handgun, blocking the way. Two robbers held their guns to the staff member's chest, ordering him to hand over the money. The two robbers searched and robbed all the 3,700 yuan in paper money and fled. The staff member reported the incident to the Fifth District Police Station, requesting an investigation. The district chief inquired in detail about the robbery and the robbers' faces and clothing. The car driver claimed that he seemed to recognize the robbers or that they were laid-off workers. The district chief felt that the car driver seemed suspicious and ordered him to be detained for investigation. The car driver is currently being held at the Fifth District Police Station.

Reason for Full Power Outage in the French Concession the Other Night 163

Mischief by a Rat

The *North-China Daily News* reports that at 8:35 PM on Sunday (the 7th), all electric lights in the French Concession went out, and were only restored at 8:50 PM. Inquiries to the electric company revealed that a rat had infiltrated the main switch due to inadequate protection, causing a short circuit between two high-voltage circuits.

Catching Adultery in the Act 164

Cheng Deyu Kicks Open the Door

Shameless Man and Woman Both Captured

Cheng Deyu, a 34-year-old native of Jiangdu, currently resides at No. 93 Daxing Back Street in the South City and works in the silk industry. He married a Miss Xu from his hometown many years ago. However, Miss Xu developed a promiscuous nature and was restless at home. Recently, she engaged in secret affairs with Jin Zhongyang, a fortune-teller from Yuyao residing nearby at No. 116 Chezhan Road. Although Cheng had heard rumors for some time, he tolerated it repeatedly due to concerns about his reputation. However, Miss Xu remained unsatisfied and, a few days ago, used the excuse to urge Cheng to take their young son back to Yangzhou first. Cheng, unable to endure any longer, secretly hid the child at a relative's house and pretended to return home. In reality, Cheng remained to investigate. Unexpectedly, Jin went to Cheng's house that very night to secretly meet with Miss Xu. Cheng then kicked open the door and caught them both naked. He immediately called for the patrol officer from No. 29 Jiangyin Street, who arrested them and took them to the Second District Police Headquarters. Chief Wang of the district initially interrogated Miss Xu, who confessed that she was 36 years old. She claimed that Jin Zhongyang owed her money, and she had repeatedly demanded repayment. Last night, he asked her to spend one night with him in exchange for clearing the debt. She said that because her husband had already returned home, she agreed to his request. When questioned, Jin Zhongyang, admitting to being 55 years old, directly confessed to having illicit relations with Miss Xu. Chief Wang, based on the confession, considered the case to involve adultery and immediately prepared documents to transfer the case to the court for trial.

French Merchant Van Lenna Fraudulently Obtains Huge Sums 165

French Consulate Sentences to Five Years Imprisonment

The *North-China Daily News* reports that French merchant Van Lenna repeatedly created false invoices and bad checks to fraudulently obtain huge sums of money from major banks in Shanghai through the practice of document against acceptance. He successively defrauded them of a total of 15,000 pounds. The French Consulate has now sentenced him to five years imprisonment and a fine of 3,000 francs, but suspended the sentence. His accomplice, Arnault, was sentenced to six months imprisonment and a fine of 1,000 francs, also with a suspended sentence of five years. The defendant was charged with fifteen counts in total. Three of these counts involved repeatedly defrauding the Bank of India and the Banque Franco-Chinoise of a total of 7,730 pounds of money obtained against bills amounting to 5,065 pounds. The other twelve counts involved inciting and assisting his employee, Arnault, to repeatedly defraud the Banque Franco-Chinoise, Hongkong and Shanghai Banking Corporation, and the Mercantile Bank of India, London and China, of 25,000 pounds of money obtained against bills amounting to 10,000 pounds. After the court hearing, the representative of the Banque Franco-Chinoise stated that between March and April of this year, the defendant repeatedly used invoices, bills of lading, and bills of exchange for shipments of European raw silk to obtain advances from the bank. By July, the defendant's company had gone bankrupt, and the drafts he issued were rejected by the drawees. Investigations revealed that the weight and packing dimensions of the European raw silk were completely inconsistent with the invoices and bills of lading. As a result, the plaintiff bank could only sell one-quarter of the advanced money. Subsequently, the liquidator of the defendant's company, accountant B. Weill, testified that 1.6 million francs were missing from the accounts and had been remitted to the defendant's brothers in Lyon, with almost no assets remaining in Shanghai. Later, representatives from the Bank of India, Hongkong and Shanghai Banking Corporation, and the Mercantile Bank of India successively described their experiences of being defrauded, which were largely similar. Finally, the defendant confessed to the fraud. He claimed that he initially created false invoices to obtain advances to cover debts of 100,000 francs owed in France in May of last year, and this gradually became a habit that he could no longer remedy, stating that he did not intend to defraud. The judge considered that this behavior damaged commercial ethics and undermined the foundation of credit instruments, and should be severely punished. He sentenced the defendant as described above, but suspended the sentence. The accomplice, Arnault, was also charged with twelve counts, but had previously fled Shanghai and failed to appear in court. He was tried in absentia and also had his sentence suspended.

Counterfeiting Discount Coupons for a Soy Sauce Store 166

Defrauding Away a Lot of Soybean Oil, Several Brothers Arrested Together

The newly opened Dingfeng Soy Sauce Store at the intersection of Zhoujiazui Road and Zhoushan Road in the Zhabei district, to attract customers, held a discount event and printed a type of special coupon, each coupon worth one yuan. Holding this coupon to purchase oil could obtain cheaper goods. The store clerk, Lu Bosheng from Suzhou, related this matter to his younger brother, Fusheng, thinking that they could take the opportunity to counterfeit the coupons to sell as imitations, thereby greatly profiting. They decided on the plan and carried it out. At first, they were not detected, and they grew bolder, issuing more and more counterfeit coupons. On the day before yesterday, from morning to noon, the soy sauce store successively received over twenty counterfeit coupons, causing them great suspicion. In the late afternoon, Wang Rensheng from Changshu, carrying two oil boxes on his shoulders, brought eleven coupons to exchange for soybean oil. Examining the coupons, the store owner, Li Qinzhou, found that none of them were genuine, so he detained Wang and reported it to the Hongkou Police Station, which dispatched detectives to arrest Wang for questioning. Wang then confessed that the coupons were made by Lu Bosheng, an employee of Dingfeng, and his younger brother, Fusheng. They then arrested Lu. Since Fusheng lived in the territory of the Second Precinct of the First District in the Chinese area, they coordinated with detectives and rushed to Fusheng's home to search it. They confiscated counterfeit coupons, stamps, and several boxes of soybean oil obtained through fraud and took them back to the police station. Fusheng was temporarily detained at the police station, awaiting a formal request from the Special District Local Court to transfer him for interrogation. The morning before yesterday, Lu Bosheng was escorted to the Special Court, where Judge Feng interrogated him and ordered him to be detained, awaiting a letter to the Municipal Security Bureau to transfer Lu Fusheng to be interrogated together.

Rickshaw Puller Dies from a Fall 167

Rickshaw puller Wu Renming, from Jiangbei, fell to the ground at 6:10 AM on the day before yesterday on Nanxun Road due to carelessness while competing with other pullers for customers and died immediately. The Hongkou Police Station, upon receiving the report, ordered detectives to investigate and transport the body to the morgue on Feilun Road for an autopsy. Yesterday morning, the Special District Local Court commissioned prosecutor Xu Mei to conduct the autopsy. Xu Mei took his seat and, based on the report from the deceased's brother, Wu Lungong, requesting to claim the body, concluded that Wu Renming had died from a fall. Since the police found no other suspicious circumstances, the body was released to his brother for burial.

Free Talk

A Word of Insight 178

— Long

Don't simply envy other people's wives for being fashionable and beautiful. They are likely anxious that they can't satisfy their loved one's desire for money.

Giving up a seat to a female passenger on the tram is indeed a virtue. However, from the perspective of new people, men may be underestimating women as weaklings.

A person who can still cry is not yet completely heartbroken. A truly heartbroken person will never let others know.

The joy obtained in favorable circumstances is not true joy. The joy obtained in adverse circumstances is true joy.

Beautiful women need money just as flowers and plants need rainwater; both are indispensable. Therefore, beautiful women and famous flowers can be said to be the exclusive property of the wealthy, and poor scholars cannot inquire.

The ancients said that it is best to drink wine until half-intoxicated, and flowers are most beautiful when they are half-bloomed. Everything in life should be viewed in this way to be interesting.

A man who truly understands equality and liberalism will never blame a woman for falling in love with someone else. Because a woman is not a toy, she has her freedom. If she doesn't love you and goes to love someone else, can you force her to love you and not love someone else?

Money obtained through schemes is difficult to accumulate. Money obtained through hard work is easy to keep.

It is not difficult for us to find a lover, but it is difficult to find a confidant.

Old Man Su Kan's Talk on Health Preservation 179

— Ma Gongyu

Mr. Zheng Sukan is seventy-one years old this year, but his body is strong and his spirit is vigorous. He looks like someone in their fifties. He has not suffered from illness for decades. When he traveled to Japan, he walked across steep mountains and climbed dangerous rocks with the agility of a young man, which was admired by people in that country. I once suspected that he had a secret recipe for health preservation, so I asked him. Mr. Zheng smiled and said, "There is no other way to preserve health than to eat less, sleep less, and work more." I sleep at 9:00 PM every night and get up at 3:00 AM, so I call myself "Night Riser." After getting up, I exercise for about five minutes, drink a little tea, and write from 4:00 AM to 6:00 AM. I eat congee for breakfast, half a bread roll for lunch, and congee for dinner. Other than that, I don't eat anything else. I work all day without feeling hungry or tired. I have been doing this for more than twenty years. I never eat any tonics. I don't like comfort in ordinary times. I have never been afraid to go out even on cold, snowy days. Sometimes, because I get up too early, the servants are not awake, so I get water, wash my face, and brew tea myself without feeling tired, and my body becomes stronger every day because of it. When night comes at the hours of Zi and Chou [11:00 PM - 3:00 AM], the subtle Yang energy begins to move, which is the time when heaven and earth generate life. People's thoughts are clearest at this time (this is Mencius's theory of night energy). If one can escape the dark slumber at this time, one's physical strength and spirit will naturally be full, and evil Qi will not easily invade. This is why I get up at night. People only know to eat more to nourish the body and indulge in leisure to nourish strength, but they don't know that nourishing the body doesn't entirely depend on food, and exercise is even more sufficient to ward off illness. This is why I eat sparingly and like to work." These famous words are enough to exhaust the ancient and modern methods of health preservation. Mr. Zheng's calligraphy is famous all over the world, and he never stops learning calligraphy every day, becoming more and more skilled as he gets older. Recently, he has also liked to write Qin seal script and cursive script, with his brush strokes surpassing his predecessors. However, Mr. Zheng himself says that he needs more time to be admired. He is so humble. Mr. Zheng commented that my seal script is the most energetic and flawless, and he also kindly wrote a preface to my clumsy engraved seal collection, praising it excessively, which makes me feel ashamed. Mr. Zheng especially praised my elder brother Mengrong's paintings as being both heavenly and man-made, praising them incessantly. His sincere encouragement of later generations is beyond what others can achieve.

Mei Lanfang's Talk on Stabbing the Tiger 180

— Yan Mang

In America, the first successful play, the American newspapers comment on this play

Mei Lanfang's previous visit to the United States was extremely successful and was recorded in the annals. The greatest power of artistic success was the play *Stabbing the Tiger*. This play tells the story of the late Ming Dynasty when Li Zicheng was approaching the capital. A princess, fearing pursuit by the bandits, had a palace maid, Zhen'e, pretend to be the princess and hide in a dry well. Later, she was found by Li Zicheng's subordinates and presented to Zicheng. Zicheng married her to General Li Guo. Li was brave and good at fighting, and everyone praised him as a "tiger." On the night of the wedding, Zhen'e took advantage of his drunkenness and killed him. Zhen'e's original intention was to assassinate Zicheng, but even though she accidentally hit the wrong target, she still regretted her wasted talent. In a fit of anger, she also committed suicide. The entire play is called *Iron Crown Picture*, and *Stabbing the Tiger* is the most exciting part of it. Mei performed this play in the United States, and it moved cities. The audience was as crowded as a wall, and there were still countless people who could not get tickets after it had been performed for a month. Its value can be known. The structure of this play is excellent, and its meaning is very profound. Furthermore, Mei's performance is delicate and moving, without any carelessness. The great praise comes with good reason. Yesterday, a friend sent me a collection of Mei's reviews in American newspapers, and I have translated a few sections about *Stabbing the Tiger* below:

The *New York Evening Post* said that Mei's performance of *Stabbing the Tiger* said, "Stabbing the Tiger is a drama with profound meaning because it is about revenge and sacrifice."

The *New York Morning Post* said, "Stabbing the Tiger is about a palace maid's revenge. The meaning of this play is similar to the modern plays *Judith of Bethulia* and *The Road to Rome*, which are quite imitative of it."

The *New York Telegraph* said, "This play, *Stabbing the Tiger*, makes it easier for us to understand and feel endless interest in it compared to other plays. The palace maid played by Mei Jun is very much like Lady Macbeth in Shakespeare's play Macbeth."

American drama critic Yang Shide said, "Chinese opera is like reality everywhere, but at the same time, it is far from reality. It is a manifestation of daily life everywhere, but what is expressed is not daily life, which is very surprising to us. Chinese opera is a very profound program that expresses the entire art."

He also said, "The thing that impressed me most about Chinese opera is the play *Stabbing the Tiger*."

The *New York Daily News* said, "Mei Jun is a person who combines 'dance,' 'acting,' and 'singing.' I have never seen hand gestures performed so beautifully on stage."

The *New York Times* said, "Mei Jun's performance is extremely pure, like a pool of clear water in the forest."

It also said, "Mei Jun's posture is solemn and beautiful, which cannot be described in words."

Yang Shide said, "Mei Jun's movements and expressions, whether it is the rest of Repose or the shocking Shock, are the essence of the most perfect and pure art. Fear, Pity, Murderous Resolution, Despair, all kinds of states can be shown on his face, and every part of his body is a manifestation of art, without ever leaving beauty."

The above-mentioned reviews show the satisfactory criticism that Mei Jun received in the United States on his previous visit.

Factory Visit to the Buliduoli [Supplement Power Lots] Manufacturing Plant 181

— Lie

Since the spread of modern medical theories in our country, the need for new medicines has been increasing day by day, and the price of medicines flowing into foreign countries every year is astonishing. Recently, the voice of promoting domestic products can be heard everywhere, but due to the limitations of economy and talent, the majority of new medicines have not been able to be manufactured domestically. The Jiufu Company created various exquisite and perfect medicines that can replace imported goods. This year, two new drugs, pure Buliduoli and Hanjiguai Buliduoli [Supplement Power Lots], are aimed at imported goods that economically invade foreign countries, so since their release, they have won the sympathy of all sectors of society. The company succeeded in producing these drugs only after much research, and previously invited the medical and pharmaceutical communities to openly visit the factory, which was highly praised and considered to be the only great pharmaceutical factory in our country. On the day before yesterday (December 6), they invited the press and people from all walks of life to visit the factory. I drove to the company's factory site on Baker Road at around 3:00 PM and saw that the visitors were already extremely crowded. I immediately signed my name and entered, and was led into the Buliduoli manufacturing workshop by a company employee. Various manufacturing machines were running, making non-stop grinding noises. Each machine was arranged in a large manufacturing room. Starting with extracting the essence of cod liver oil, various medicines and procedures were successively added. The process was transmitted from machine A to machine B, and then from machine B to machine C, passing through more than twenty times until Buliduoli was manufactured. The entire process did not use manual labor and relied entirely on the latest scientific methods and new-style machines. It can also be seen that the progress of our country's pharmaceutical industry is very different from what it was a few years ago. All kinds of machines were labeled with their names, including a total of more than ten kinds of machines, such as a fully automatic mixer, a lifting machine, a centrifugal separation clarifying machine, a vacuum distillation machine, a cooling machine, a suction machine, a washing machine, a finishing machine, a filter press, an emulsifying machine, a combining machine, and a mixing machine. After visiting the Buliduoli manufacturing workshop, we turned to the second room and saw the machines for manufacturing Bailingji [hundred spirits base] tonic pills and for manufacturing Shengdan [birth pill] pills were all working. It was heard that working eight hours a day could produce 1,200 bottles of pure Buliduoli, 1,200 bottles of Hanjiguai Buliduoli, 500,000 pieces of Bailingji, and 2 million Shengdan pills. On that day, about 3,000 people from all walks of life came to visit. Fortunately, they came and went continuously, so it did not feel too crowded. There were also sixty or seventy people from the press. At around 5:00 PM, the company prepared Muscat tea and refreshments in the tea room on the second floor for a brief chat with the press. During the conversation, I heard people talk about how, since the drug stores refused to sell foreign goods, the demand for the company's Buliduoli had increased even more. Also, at the turn of autumn and winter, there were many patients with coughs and lung diseases, so the sales of Hanjiguai Buliduoli were especially smooth. It was heard that foreign merchants were very alarmed by this situation and planned to contact our country's drug merchants with huge sums of money, hoping to continue selling foreign goods. However, we take patriotism as the premise and should not be tempted by meager money. After the tea and refreshments were finished, I returned and recorded it.

Travel Notes from Nanyang (94) 182

— Linghua

I was happy to ask for directions, but I was struggling to find someone to translate Hindi. From five o'clock until eight o'clock, I began to sit again, and I repeated various styles of worship in the four directions, muttering with my head prostrating to the fire. His whole body was covered in ash. How strange. I asked someone to translate and asked him, and he replied that there were books. When I asked again, he did not answer directly, but spoke in various languages and told me to come closer. He put a few pieces of fruit pulp in my hand and gave me a lotus flower that was about to bloom. Then he ordered me to take a pinch of ash from the fire with my hand and follow him. He also ordered me to put the ash on my face and smear it on. I realized that he was going to use magic to make me believe in his religion. I told him directly that I was unwilling. He still had words, so I said goodbye. The ash-throwing heretics can practice austerities, not wear clothes, and worship fire as their teacher. The Kasyapa brothers, disciples of the Buddha, had a total of 1,250 disciples, all of whom were heretics who worshipped fire. The reason why they were conquered by the Buddha was that people in ancient times had to keep the fire burning day and night because it was difficult to continue the fire if it was extinguished, so they thought it was a god of light and guarded it. This eventually became a kind of belief. Evolved people changed it to lighting lamps and candles. This school is not progressive and still adheres to ancient methods, evolving into religion. The Book of Changes says that Li is fire. India has earth, water, fire, and wind. Various heretics explain the origin of all things, and the early philosophers of Greece also used water, fire, wind, etc. to explain it. The basis of heretics who worship fire is not without reason, but they can practice austerities. But it is also not economical. They eat one catty of milk a day, which is very expensive. Their consumption of firewood must be at least two yuan. Their daily life must cost at least three yuan. Then, what is the point of this asceticism? The income of a worker is not enough to pay for it. No wonder their bodies are very fat and plump. In short, it is not appropriate to eat without plowing. In today's enlightened world of economics, all gods and ghosts should reduce their powers to engage in work. Tolstoy often said that he laughed at the missionaries of the religious family, saying that the head can work and should be able to eat. He placed the priests in the upstairs for several days without giving them food, so they cried loudly and fell down, saying that this was Xu Xing and Geng Ying's group mocking the Confucians.

European Tour Correspondence (88) 183

— Liu Haisu

Pilgrimage to Italy Diary

(3) Ten Days in Rome (11)

Day Three — Trajan's Column — San Pietro in Vincoli Basilica —

Anyone who travels to Italy and sets foot in the streets of Rome will always feel the different flavors of the remains of the Roman era and the Renaissance. After seeing many bathhouses, triumphal arches, monuments, or large buildings of temples and palaces, and further entering the halls and rooms to observe the sculptures and paintings, one can especially recognize the differences in their primary mission and artistic elements. The Roman era was busy developing national power, and its characteristic was the military-state strategy of emphasizing practicality and real benefits. Therefore, the artworks of that time only had "necessity" and "utility," lacking pure artistic creative desire, thus becoming true realism. This is why the architecture and sculpture of that time were mostly assembly halls, large bathhouses, circular theaters, triumphal arches, memorial columns, bridges, and aqueducts, the remains of which are still found throughout Rome. Although the Renaissance, which began in the fourteenth century, claimed to trace classical art, its spiritual essence still lay in the evolution of Christian culture over thousands of years. In terms of architecture, from underground tombs to Basilica, to Romanesque, to Gothic, to Byzantium, it has been developed all the way to the Renaissance style. Renaissance architecture spread from Italy to Europe at that time. They also destroyed the relics of ancient times and took those stone materials and sculptures to decorate tombs and churches — for example, the marble columns of the Roman St. Peter's Basilica came from the tomb of Hadrianus, and the bronze doors of the Lateran Basilica were moved from the Baths of Caracalla — Rome's largest building, St. Peter's Basilica, the world's largest cathedral, was also completed during this period.

Slowly bypass Trajan's Column Square and the Colosseum, and suddenly ascend a few dozen stone steps to a plateau. The majestic and extraordinary structure of the San Pietro in Vincoli temple stands in front of the square. This is the main relic of the Basilica style built in the fourth century, which is different from the style of Renaissance architecture. Since Emperor Constantine designated Christianity as the state religion, Christians walked out of the underground Catacombs and built Basilica churches on the ground. Later, Basilica architecture was directly inherited by Romanesque architecture. On the other hand, it moved to Byzantium due to the eastward migration of Emperor Constantine the Great, and evolved into Byzantine art.

San Pietro in Vincoli temple is a rectangular building with gorgeous mosaic floors inside. In 1506, Pope Julius II commissioned Michelangelo to build his tomb here. Originally, Michelangelo planned to create dozens of statues like Moses, using the majestic ideal possessed by the power and solemnity of the Sistine Chapel ceiling. Unfortunately, not long after the work began, it was terminated due to the slander of the architect Bramante, which is a huge loss to humanity that Romain Rolland lamented in distress.

The Moses statue is now on the right side of the altar. When we look at it, we feel that the statue is filled with irrepressible anger, with bulging muscles on the face, expressing a sublime and great spirit, simply possessing the might of the Alps.

The forward bean cake market saw a good performance yesterday, originating from the extremely active trading of the May contract, especially attracting attention from inland buyers. Currently, continuous good news reports and rising margins have boosted confidence, resulting in a strong market in the afternoon. The April contract opened at 1 tael, 5 qian, and 4 fen, up 1.5 fen. The May contract opened at 1 tael, 5 qian, 5 fen, and 7.5 li, also up 1.75 li.

The forward soybean market turned slightly firm because inland buyers believe that the harvest in Anhui province along the Yangtze River this year will be very good, so they are mostly bearish. However, local trading houses are shifting their focus to Dalian, so the market outlook is good. Because observations differ, there is not much trading between the two sides. The market is only slightly better by one or two fen compared to the previous weekend.

Sugar Market: Raw Sugar and White Sugar Break the 8-Tael Barrier 199

The Shanghai Factory's white ice sugar price rises by 2 qian.

Taikoo Sugar releases 4,000 bags.

Raw sugar and white sugar are offered at 800 tons.

The market is quite good, and the upward trend continues unabated.

The public association market division panel took into account the surge in margins, the higher exchange rate, and stronger sentiment. The initial market price for Dutch sugar raw sugar and white sugar was 8 taels, and the sentiment was still strong, rising to 8 taels and 5 fen, an increase of 1 qian compared to the previous day. The market was also strong. Medium white sugar No. 20 reached a high of 7 taels and 2 qian from 7 taels and 1 qian. Fine sugar No. 8 was priced at 8 taels, 1 qian, and 2.5 fen, and Dutch red sugar No. 8 was priced at 6 taels and 6 qian. No. 9 was priced at 6 taels and 7 qian, and No. 10 was priced at 6 taels and 8 qian to 8.5 qian. The market was also quite firm. Japanese sugar imports and exports were chaotic and unusual. N mark reached 8 taels and 3 qian. TK mark ranged from 8 taels, 1 qian and 5 fen to 2 qian and 5 fen. YT mark ranged from 8 taels, 1 qian to 1 qian and 7.5 fen. Although transactions were not very active, the market sentiment was extremely good, and the confidence was firm, with a strong sense of continued growth. Taikoo Sugar continued to release spot goods. B mark was priced at 8 taels and 5 qian. The Shanghai Gang had purchased three truckloads. TK mark, etc., were also fully available. In addition, 4,000 bags of ready-to-load goods were released, with B mark accounting for 70%, 2,800 bags priced at 6 taels and 5.5 qian, and CW mark accounting for 30%, 1,200 bags priced at 6 taels and 4 qian. The new tax increase still feels attractive. Raw sugar and white sugar for sale include 800 tons of Dutch sugar offered by Hua Xin Company, arriving at the end of the month, priced at 5 yuan and 8 jiao in Dutch currency. The Shanghai factory's white ice sugar offered 300 to 500 bags, with a price increase of 2 qian, with Ren mark priced at 10 taels and 8 qian and Qian mark priced at 10 taels and 7 qian. At the same time, the China factory also followed the market and offered sales, and the market was also firm. According to Shantou news, the new green sugar of the national product has already appeared in Chenghai, with a price of 13 yuan in Shantou, equivalent to about 7 taels and 5 qian in Shanghai. Because the price of Binghua green sugar is high, there are few inquiries. Therefore, it is not cost-effective for trading houses to transport it to Shanghai, so it cannot be delivered immediately to meet the needs.

There is Talk of a Price Increase for Wufu White Ice 200

Wufu White Ice has seen strong sales recently, with each shipment selling out quickly. Currently, due to rising raw material prices and the upcoming tax increase on January 1 next year, the cost will inevitably increase. Based on the current market price of raw materials, it is difficult to make a profit. Therefore, the factory sent a telegram to Shanghai yesterday, instructing the manager to hold firm and not to exchange at the original price. It is estimated that it will open at 2 qian higher than the previous market. The goods in transit should arrive in Shanghai today.

Russia Purchases 90,000 Dan of Japanese Tea 201

According to reliable sources, Russian tea purchasing agencies have recently purchased no less than 90,000 dan of Japanese tea in Vladivostok, with a price of about 25 taels per dan in Chinese silver. The most important condition of the negotiated result is a one-year grace period for payment. This move has greatly impacted the sales of Chinese tea. However, the quality of Japanese tea is not good, and it must be combined with purchased Chinese tea before it can be transported to Russia for sale.

Social News

The Women's Movement in Near Eastern Islamic Countries 203

— Yi Kang

In the past, women in Near Eastern Islamic countries were confined to their homes, much like women in old China. However, since the successive national revolutions in countries such as Turkey, Egypt, Persia, and Afghanistan, women have been liberated along with the revolutions. With their self-awareness, the women's movement has risen in various countries in the Near East.

Therefore, they are now coming out of their homes and going to public schools, public courts, dance halls, and even entering the world of business. This has become a common phenomenon from Turkey to Arabia, from Egypt to Afghanistan. Western women are joining them in international friendships, and they are going to Europe to participate in international women's conferences. From observing the phenomena in women's circles in various Near Eastern countries, the trend of Europe is evident in Turkey, a steady progress is evident in Egypt, a determinism is evident in Syria where women are debating, and a clash between old etiquette and new ideas is evident in Persia, Arabia, and Afghanistan. However, everywhere a surge of awakening has arisen along with the revolutionary movements in various Near Eastern countries.

The recent Near East Women's Conference held in Damascus, Syria, was an unprecedented grand event in the Near East. Representatives from various Near Eastern countries delivered speeches using languages other than Asian languages. Representatives from the European International Women's Federation used French, the Persian representative used English, and the Turkish representative used fluent Arabic. The conference resolved many proposals, and the three most important goals were to implement monogamy, abolish concubinage, give women the right to choose their husbands, and abolish asceticism.

The veils of Islamic women have been completely abolished in Turkey. They no longer wear veils and are no longer confined to the black bars (Haerem) created for them by men. This movement to abolish women's veils began in 1912 when a woman in Constantinople abolished her veil, walked on the street, and gave speeches to women. The women's movement that arose along with the Turkish national revolution has achieved the complete abolition of women's veils. Kemal, the leader of the Turkish Nationalist Party, who practically gave women freedom in politics during the women's movement, had a great deal of influence. Therefore, modern Turkish women are striving to accept European experience. They not only want to go to school to gain knowledge, but also to work to gain economic independence. They want to find husbands who are of their own will. They want to stand alone and plan all their plans. They go to coffee shops and dance halls to practice social interaction publicly. They read the works of Lottie Russell, Shaw, and others. They wear Europeanized costumes in front of magazine or newspaper beauty judges. They devote themselves to drama and other art movements. They have broken the old Turkish model and almost completely imitated the American expatriate girls. Turkish girls are considered the happiest, freest, and most independent people among their Muslim sisters.

The future of Egyptian Islamic women is not as smooth as that of Turkish women, and thorns are often found on their road to liberation. Orthodox Muslims believe that there is no clear record in the "Quran" that women should wear hats. Therefore, after the publication of "The Emancipation of Woman" by the leader of the national movement, Gui Si Amin (Zasimin Amin), more than a dozen books were immediately published to resist him. However, Gui Si Amin had already grasped the hearts of many people, and even at Al-Azhar University in Cairo, he had his students. He advocated reforming marriage, reforming divorce and polygamy laws, advocating equality for women, and advocating the abolition of women's veils, which caused great opposition at the time. However, later even Rushdi Pasha's first wife also wrote two books in support of Gui Xin Amin's claims.

After the efforts of many pioneers of the women's movement, today several famous magazines in Cairo, Egypt, have women serving as editors. The most famous female writer is Nary Ziade. She is a Christian girl from Mount Lebanon in Syria. Her home in Cairo is a magnet for men and women of various religions in the city. She uses the pen name Mary to publish her articles on women's issues and literary works. Before long, she became a powerful authority in the women's movement, not only in Egypt, but her works have become the only reading material for readers in the Arabic-speaking world.

In Syria, Muslim women also participate in social affairs and literary and artistic celebrations. However, the abolition of veils is not as courageous as that of Turkish women. Although they oppose the old traditions, they ultimately do not obtain the freedom they expect. Therefore, they do not even have the courage to take off their veils. It is even more difficult to obtain economic status like Turkish girls. Only in clothing have Syrian women adopted the style of the Paris Boulevord. When walking on the street, they often attract people's attention. However, recently a group of women who admire European fashion have also attempted to overthrow all the old etiquettes. In Damascus, that bastion of etiquette, someone has already raised the banner of resistance. Moreover, the women's conference held in Damascus recently has taken steps to follow all the great achievements of Turkish women in its proposals, and they will surely be able to obtain a bright future.

Therefore, today women in Syria, Palestine, and Iraq (Iraq) are all engaged in various business endeavors. Whether they are Christians, Muslims, or Druze (Iruse) from Mount Lebanon, they are all working together to cultivate their economic status. Although they differ in religious beliefs, they all agree on economic and political organization and acquisition. They all recognize education as the only good tool for success. Therefore, the education movement that has risen in the four major cities of Jerusalem, Damascus, Beirut, and Baghdad is much stronger than the Paris fashion movement. Twenty years ago, there were only twenty Muslim girls engaged in reading in Beirut. However, according to statistics released by the Education Committee today, this city alone has exceeded one thousand people.

Beirut is the leading center of education in recent times. There are many local and foreign schools, colleges, and universities, and the style is better than any city in the world. However, before the European War, women's schools were entirely established by foreign churches. Muslim parents opposed sending their daughters to heretical church schools. After the European War, all foreign church schools were closed. Syrian woman Mary Kassab (Marv Kassab) opened a local school in an English church. In a few years, the number of students increased from twenty to three hundred, causing a passion for women's education in neighboring countries. Until today, in Palestine, Iraq, Damascus, and all Arabic-speaking countries, Muslim, Christian, and Bannon mountain Druze women who are engaged in various businesses all come to Mary Kassab's Ahlyah School to study. She has no secret of success. Although knowledge and enthusiasm are praised by others, the fact that it is run by Syrians is the first key secret.

Youth Corner

Before the Wine Vessel 204

— Su Ling

On Sunday night, Zhi Ren and I walked out of a small movie theater. The tears brought on by the tragic story in the film were still moistening our eyes, and our hearts were surging with endless melancholy. So we both felt like having some wine.

I meant to find a small Western bar, but Zhi Ren wanted to eat some Chinese food. After walking to the end of a quiet street, we entered an old-fashioned Chinese restaurant. Like the European Cafe, it was filled with all kinds of people, so we could hear all kinds of news inside. Places like this have a considerable history, and all the decorations and tableware are still in the style of the old century. This is precisely why it has those customers, and those customers also have a history with it.

Amidst the clamorous talking, arguing, fist-fighting roars, waiter responses, chopstick clatter, glass clinks… and the mixed smell of wine, meat, and various dishes… Zhi Ren and I found half a table to sit at.

So we slowly sipped the white rose in our glasses.

"Ah, since I came back from the south, it's been almost two months, and I've only had wine once, at a relative's house with some old gentlemen, two glasses of aged wine. This is the second time I've had wine. It's strange, I never have the mood to drink alone. Zhi Ren, you can imagine how lonely my life has been."

"But my loneliness is simply turning me into a bell in an empty hall."

"But you still have groups of young students to talk to. From the souls of these little ones, you will no longer be lonely."

"Ah, have you ever experienced the terrible mechanical nature of that kind of life?"

"Alas, I'm just hoping to have such a regular life, otherwise my neurasthenia will have no way to be cured. This illness makes me suffer."

So I raised my glass. I knew very well that the liquid in the glass would have a worse effect on my illness, but I had no right to stop it from pouring into my stomach.

Silence lasted for a while because our mouths were stuffed.

"The pain of life often makes me recall the joys of the past and become pessimistic," Zhi Ren said.

"This is the greatest crisis for young people. Zhi Ren, the pain of my life is even greater than yours. Memories of the past are unavoidable, but I am confident that I am not pessimistic at all. I am still pursuing things. You see, since I left school, my passion has remained."

"I believe that very much."

"Like Zhi Chang, who lives in Sichuan, his letters are always full of sentences saying that the past is unbearable to look back on. My replies are all urging him to rekindle his passion, but there is no way. The burdens of life are the greatest scourge for young people. People like us who have no wives and children are still considered lucky."

Zhi Ren only sighed.

"Sometimes thinking about the past is indeed interesting. Zhi Ren, do you remember when we first met in Nanjing?"

"Yes, the friends in Nanjing back then, there's no news from them now."

"At that time, you first lived with Zou Xiaoying and the others in the picture mounting shop on Huapai Lou, and later moved to Hanximen."

"Alas, I don't know where they went."

"He was completely a child."

"We moved from Hanximen to the sports field again."

"In short, that year passed by in a daze."

"We can say we were destined to be together. Later, we came to Shanghai together again."

"Coming to Shanghai, we met Zhi Chang and the others again."

"Ha, that winter, Zhi Chang pursued Kai very enthusiastically."

"Like Zhi Chang, he is always a lucky person. Friends generally say that. 'Only Zhi Chang is maintaining his relationship with K very peacefully.' But because the time is not long, Zhi Chang is good at flattering women, but if love passes by like this, peacefully, it can indeed save regret in the future."

"So, Zhi Chang returned to Sichuan. How can a crazy person like you talk about love?"

"The failure or success of love doesn't matter, but I made so many enemies because of it. At first, it was Lao Li, and finally, there was Lao Guan. I strongly deny their attitude."

"Although Zhi Chang had a good beginning and a good end with Kai, your relationship with Kai did have a passionate process at one point. I'm afraid Zhi Chang can't compare to you."

"Precisely because of this, once love reaches its climax, it will sooner or later lead to a possible rupture. In fact, everything is like that."

"According to general talk, that's all because you make women too disappointed in love. Although I left Shanghai in the latter half of last year and didn't see your ending."

"I fully admit my faults. I once swore that if possible, I would repent to her, ah."

"Yes, now your life and attitude have changed from movement to stillness, from constant jumping to silence. That's largely due to her influence."

"Of course, but this trip to the north also gave me a lot of stimulation. However, the surface is still, but perhaps the heart is even more turbulent. Do you believe it?"

"Your trip to the north was also due to her influence."

"The lack of order in life in the north made me feel extreme pain, so I hurriedly returned to the south."

"Ah, thinking about it, if you hadn't met Lao Xu at the entrance of the New World, I'm afraid you wouldn't have known that I was also in Shanghai, and I wouldn't have known that you would be back from the north. When I left Shanghai and returned to my hometown for half a year, I was given a great lesson. Before, I always believed that if I couldn't make a living outside, I could always go home. Who knew that reality is the opposite of this idea. There will be no place for me to eat at home anymore. So I can only come to Shanghai and do this mechanical thing. Fortunately, Lao Fan kept it for me."

"Thinking about Lao Fan, it's also unfortunate that his dream of being an official has been realized again."

"He wrote in a letter that he lost more than 3,000 yuan. He only did a month or two of being an official and will soon come to Shanghai."

……………………

"Ah, these past events, these past events..."

So I sipped the last drop of wine. Zhi Ren smiled and said,

Page 22

"If we imagine the future, what will we be like in a year or ten years?"

"Either surrounded by children or remaining a bachelor forever. In short, I will definitely be a bachelor."

The Freshman Society at Tongji 205

— Shi Yong

Tongji, which has always been filled with a dull atmosphere, has seen an unusual level of activity in academic organizations this semester. The ordinary and gloomy school life of the past has suddenly taken on a vibrant momentum. Recently, the emergence of the Freshman Society is truly an alarm bell in the dull atmosphere, a new phenomenon in student organization.

The "Freshman Society" was originally named "Green Society." This was the temporary name used before the official establishment of the general meeting. Later, it was changed to "Freshman Society" after being passed by all members. The intention of this naming is to "abandon the dull old life and create a new life for the future."

Although the society has few members, the spirit of unity and perseverance has not diminished slightly due to the small number of people. They are still sparing no effort in promoting the society's affairs, so the society's future is truly immeasurable. Moreover, even in the midst of busy coursework, they are still working hard to publish the first issue of the wall newspaper, which was published last Wednesday. The newspaper contained the following words:

"Because we are dissatisfied with the ordinariness and monotony of this life, the dull and suffocating atmosphere, and even more unwilling to decline in this way, we have organized this 'Freshman Society' to seek the connection of feelings and the unity of spirit among students so that this ordinary and boring school life can be improved. At the same time, we further hope that in the future, we can contribute to all students, build for the school, fulfill our responsibilities to society, and assume the mission of the times."

From this, the general spirit can be seen.

It is heard that the second issue will be full of short, concise, and interesting texts to entertain readers and is now scheduled to be published this Friday.

The Crisis of Youth in Hunan and Jiangxi Provinces 206

— Luo Yehong

Since the National Revolutionary Army launched its campaign, the millions of civilians in Hunan and Jiangxi provinces have been in the midst of artillery fire every day. In addition, due to the recent looting by bandits, the two provinces have become desolate, with millions of people fleeing and starving to death or freezing to death every day. The facts in Changsha and Ji'an can be imagined from the suffering of the people in these two provinces.

Needless to say, the finances of the two provinces are very difficult. What slaughter tax, brokerage tax, and post-disaster donation are collected every month to supply government expenses, military expenses, and education expenses? Only four or five percent is paid out each month. The schools that have already been opened are in jeopardy. Schools that have been burned down by bandits, of course, cannot be opened. Better professors have run to Tianjin and Shanghai. The economy of the society is bankrupt, and a group of suffering people cannot even seek food and clothing for themselves. How can they have money to send their children to school? The path of reading for these tens of thousands of young people is blocked.

Since the path of reading for young people is blocked, having read some books and knowing a few words, they can only run to the political world to seek a position. Who knew that in the current political world, one cannot get a job without an introduction? Moreover, there are mostly youth who have become Red and the government does not recognize youth seeking jobs. This road is also unworkable.

Young people who have no books to read and no jobs to seek can only open a small shop in the city to escape disaster and make a living if their families have a little money. The number of small shops in Nanchang and Changsha is increasing every day, but the population in the market is declining. Apart from buying daily necessities, who else buys odds and ends? Moreover, with so many shops, business is scattered. Young people have no experience, so most of them lose money. In addition, the life of holding a small room and managing the accounts has no fun at all. They are unwilling to take this road.

Young people coming out of schools mostly have teacher-student relationships in the education field and can only try to get a position as an elementary school teacher or a middle school clerk. There are only twenty or thirty elementary schools in the city, and most of the rural elementary schools have been burned down. Tens of thousands of young people are competing for twenty or thirty positions. Where is there enough to distribute? The road of education is also unworkable.

Young people closed in by high walls have no way to make a living and can only take two downward roads:

The first road: Suicide

The second road: Becoming a bandit

Recently, newspaper reports of youth suicide can often be seen in Hunan and Jiangxi provinces. Aren't the bandits in these two provinces now mostly young people under the age of thirty being used by others? It is truly a pity that these tens of thousands of brave and promising citizens are being sacrificed in this way.

If we want to rescue the youth in these two provinces now, the first step is for the government to fundamentally find ways to provide relief. There are many methods of relief, such as establishing:

(1) Student Loan Offices: Students who truly have no money to study or students who have no money due to natural disasters can be proven by the local government and given a loan for tuition.

(2) Student Job Placement Offices: Students who have just come out of school have vague and ignorant knowledge of all the paths in society. The government should introduce jobs based on their school performance and personality to avoid wandering.

(3) Implementing work-study education: All the daily work and employees in the school can be handled by students, and the money can be given to students to study, or printing plants and manufacturing plants can be set up in the school for students to work in their spare time.

In addition to this, there are many things that can be done to provide relief to young people, as long as the government plans and implements them, it will be of great benefit to the country and society. Otherwise, if this continues, the future is unimaginable.
